/* Document
   ========================================================================== */

/**
 * 1. Correct the line height in all browsers.
 * 2. Prevent adjustments of font size after orientation changes in iOS.
 */

html {
  line-height: 1.15; /* 1 */
  -webkit-text-size-adjust: 100%; /* 2 */
}

/* Sections
   ========================================================================== */

/**
 * Remove the margin in all browsers.
 */

body {
  margin: 0;
}

/**
 * Render the `main` element consistently in IE.
 */

main {
  display: block;
}

/**
 * Correct the font size and margin on `h1` elements within `section` and
 * `article` contexts in Chrome, Firefox, and Safari.
 */

h1 {
  font-size: 2em;
  margin: 0.67em 0;
}

/* Grouping content
   ========================================================================== */

/**
 * 1. Add the correct box sizing in Firefox.
 * 2. Show the overflow in Edge and IE.
 */

hr {
  box-sizing: content-box; /* 1 */
  height: 0; /* 1 */
  overflow: visible; /* 2 */
}

/**
 * 1. Correct the inheritance and scaling of font size in all browsers.
 * 2. Correct the odd `em` font sizing in all browsers.
 */

pre {
  font-family: monospace, monospace; /* 1 */
  font-size: 1em; /* 2 */
}

/* Text-level semantics
   ========================================================================== */

/**
 * Remove the gray background on active links in IE 10.
 */

a {
  background-color: transparent;
}

/**
 * 1. Remove the bottom border in Chrome 57-
 * 2. Add the correct text decoration in Chrome, Edge, IE, Opera, and Safari.
 */

abbr[title] {
  border-bottom: none; /* 1 */
  text-decoration: underline; /* 2 */
  text-decoration: underline dotted; /* 2 */
}

/**
 * Add the correct font weight in Chrome, Edge, and Safari.
 */

b,
strong {
  font-weight: bolder;
}

/**
 * 1. Correct the inheritance and scaling of font size in all browsers.
 * 2. Correct the odd `em` font sizing in all browsers.
 */

code,
kbd,
samp {
  font-family: monospace, monospace; /* 1 */
  font-size: 1em; /* 2 */
}

/**
 * Add the correct font size in all browsers.
 */

small {
  font-size: 80%;
}

/**
 * Prevent `sub` and `sup` elements from affecting the line height in
 * all browsers.
 */

sub,
sup {
  font-size: 75%;
  line-height: 0;
  position: relative;
  vertical-align: baseline;
}

sub {
  bottom: -0.25em;
}

sup {
  top: -0.5em;
}

/* Embedded content
   ========================================================================== */

/**
 * Remove the border on images inside links in IE 10.
 */

img {
  border-style: none;
}

/* Forms
   ========================================================================== */

/**
 * 1. Change the font styles in all browsers.
 * 2. Remove the margin in Firefox and Safari.
 */

button,
input,
optgroup,
select,
textarea {
  font-family: inherit; /* 1 */
  font-size: 100%; /* 1 */
  line-height: 1.15; /* 1 */
  margin: 0; /* 2 */
}

/**
 * Show the overflow in IE.
 * 1. Show the overflow in Edge.
 */

button,
input { /* 1 */
  overflow: visible;
}

/**
 * Remove the inheritance of text transform in Edge, Firefox, and IE.
 * 1. Remove the inheritance of text transform in Firefox.
 */

button,
select { /* 1 */
  text-transform: none;
}

/**
 * Correct the inability to style clickable types in iOS and Safari.
 */

button,
[type="button"],
[type="reset"],
[type="submit"] {
  -webkit-appearance: button;
}

/**
 * Remove the inner border and padding in Firefox.
 */

button::-moz-focus-inner,
[type="button"]::-moz-focus-inner,
[type="reset"]::-moz-focus-inner,
[type="submit"]::-moz-focus-inner {
  border-style: none;
  padding: 0;
}

/**
 * Restore the focus styles unset by the previous rule.
 */

button:-moz-focusring,
[type="button"]:-moz-focusring,
[type="reset"]:-moz-focusring,
[type="submit"]:-moz-focusring {
  outline: 1px dotted ButtonText;
}

/**
 * Correct the padding in Firefox.
 */

fieldset {
  padding: 0.35em 0.75em 0.625em;
}

/**
 * 1. Correct the text wrapping in Edge and IE.
 * 2. Correct the color inheritance from `fieldset` elements in IE.
 * 3. Remove the padding so developers are not caught out when they zero out
 *    `fieldset` elements in all browsers.
 */

legend {
  box-sizing: border-box; /* 1 */
  color: inherit; /* 2 */
  display: table; /* 1 */
  max-width: 100%; /* 1 */
  padding: 0; /* 3 */
  white-space: normal; /* 1 */
}

/**
 * Add the correct vertical alignment in Chrome, Firefox, and Opera.
 */

progress {
  vertical-align: baseline;
}

/**
 * Remove the default vertical scrollbar in IE 10+.
 */

textarea {
  overflow: auto;
}

/**
 * 1. Add the correct box sizing in IE 10.
 * 2. Remove the padding in IE 10.
 */

[type="checkbox"],
[type="radio"] {
  box-sizing: border-box; /* 1 */
  padding: 0; /* 2 */
}

/**
 * Correct the cursor style of increment and decrement buttons in Chrome.
 */

[type="number"]::-webkit-inner-spin-button,
[type="number"]::-webkit-outer-spin-button {
  height: auto;
}

/**
 * 1. Correct the odd appearance in Chrome and Safari.
 * 2. Correct the outline style in Safari.
 */

[type="search"] {
  -webkit-appearance: textfield; /* 1 */
  outline-offset: -2px; /* 2 */
}

/**
 * Remove the inner padding in Chrome and Safari on macOS.
 */

[type="search"]::-webkit-search-decoration {
  -webkit-appearance: none;
}

/**
 * 1. Correct the inability to style clickable types in iOS and Safari.
 * 2. Change font properties to `inherit` in Safari.
 */

::-webkit-file-upload-button {
  -webkit-appearance: button; /* 1 */
  font: inherit; /* 2 */
}

   ========================================================================== */

details {
  display: block;
}

 * Add the correct display in all browsers.
 */

summary {
  display: list-item;
}

<script type="text/javascript">
  (function (retailrocket) {
    'use strict';

    var waitFor = function (exitCondition, callback, force, opts) {
      var checkCount = (opts && opts.checkCount) || 100;
      var timeout = (opts && opts.timeout) || 1000;

      (function check() {
        var result = exitCondition();
        if (result) {
          callback(result);
          return;
        }

        if (checkCount === 0) {
          if (force) {
            callback();
          }
          return;
        }

        checkCount -= 1;
        setTimeout(check, timeout);
      }());
    };
    
    var SwiperModel = function (setting) {
      var $widget = setting.widget;
      var swiperSeector = '.rr-swiper-container';
      var source = 'https://rrstatic.retailrocket.net/widget/plugins/rrswiper/rrswiper.min.js';
      var itemsCount = $widget.getAttribute('data-number-of-rendered-items');

      function checkloop(paramsSlider) {
        var modSetting = paramsSlider;

        if (modSetting.loop == true) {
          for (var point in modSetting.breakpoints) {
            if (itemsCount <= modSetting.breakpoints[point].slidesPerView) {
              modSetting.breakpoints[point].loop = false;
            } else {
              modSetting.breakpoints[point].loop = true;
            }
          }
        }

        return modSetting;
      }

      function render(swiperLibrary) {
        var SwiperParams = checkloop(setting.settingSwiper);
        var $rrContainer = $widget.querySelector(swiperSeector);
        var rrSwiper = swiperLibrary == 'RRSwiper' ? new RRSwiper($rrContainer, SwiperParams) : new Swiper($rrContainer, SwiperParams);

        rrSwiper
          .on('init', function () {
          var $imgError = $widget.querySelectorAll('.rr-swiper-slide:not(.swiper-slide-duplicate) img');
          var counter = 0;
          var indexImg = [];

          $imgError.forEach(function (img) {
            img.onerror = function () {
              var $slideItem = img.closest('.rr-swiper-slide');
              var $slideSiblings = $slideItem.parentNode.querySelectorAll('.rr-swiper-slide:not(.swiper-slide-duplicate)');
              indexImg.push($slideItem.getAttribute('data-swiper-slide-index'));

              if ($imgError.length == counter) {
                rrSwiper.removeSlide(indexImg);
              }
            };
            counter++;
          });
          $widget.classList.add('rr-active');
        })
          .on('observerUpdate', function () {
          rrSwiper.resize.resizeHandler();
        });
        rrSwiper.init();
      }

      function getScript() {
        var swiperJs = document.createElement('script');
        var getElemScript = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
        swiperJs.async = 1;

        if (!window.Swiper && !window.RRSwiper) {
          swiperJs.onload = swiperJs.onreadystatechange = function(_, isAbort) {
            if (isAbort || !swiperJs.readyState || /loaded|complete/.test(swiperJs.readyState) ) {
              swiperJs.onload = swiperJs.onreadystatechange = null;
              swiperJs = undefined;

              if (!isAbort) setTimeout(render('RRSwiper'), 0);
            }
          };

          swiperJs.src = source;
          getElemScript.parentNode.insertBefore(swiperJs, getElemScript);
        } else {
          var versionSwiper = window.hasOwnProperty('RRSwiper') ? 'RRSwiper' : 'Swiper';
          render(versionSwiper);
        }
      }

      this.getScript = getScript;
    };

    function getItems(requireProducts, callback) {
      retailrocket.items.get(
        retailrocket.api.getPartnerId(),
        requireProducts,
        ['1'],
        callback
      );
    }
    
    function filterDouble(array) {
      var ids = array.map(function (item) {
        return item.ItemId;
      });

      return array.filter(function (item, index) {
        return ids.indexOf(item.ItemId) === index;
      });
    }
    
    if (!('duplicates' in retailrocket.modules)) {
      retailrocket.setModule('duplicates', [], function () {
        var savedIds = [];
        var paramName = 'ItemId';

        function has(id) {
          return savedIds.indexOf(id) !== -1;
        }

        function add(id) {
          savedIds = savedIds.concat(id);
        }

        function remove(id) {
          var ids = [].concat(id);

          savedIds = savedIds.filter(function (savedId) {
            return ids.indexOf(savedId) === -1;
          });
        }

        function filter(recom) {
          if (!recom[paramName]) {
            return true;
          }

          if (!has(recom[paramName])) {
            add(recom[paramName]);
            return true;
          }

          return false;
        }

        function filteredCount(recoms) {
          return recoms.reduce(function (acc, recom) {
            return acc + (has(recom[paramName]) ? 1 : 0);
          }, 0);
        }

        function getItems() {
          return savedIds.slice();
        }

        return {
          has: has,
          add: add,
          remove: remove,
          filter: filter,
          filteredCount: filteredCount,
          getItems: getItems,
        };
      });
    }

      function add2cart(btn, n, id, step) {
        if (step) {
          n = Number(step) * Number(n);
        }
        var qnt = event.target.closest('.rr-item__actions').querySelector('.control-qnt');
        
        if (btn.classList.contains('rr-item__actions-buy')) {
          btn.closest('.rr-item__actions').classList.add('added');
          qnt.innerHTML = Math.round((Number(qnt.innerHTML) + n)*100)/100;
          window.rrAddToBasket(id, qnt.innerHTML);
        } else {
          if (n == 1 || n == step) {
            qnt.innerHTML = Math.round((Number(qnt.innerHTML) + n)*100)/100;
            window.rrAddToBasket(id, qnt.innerHTML);
          }
          if (n == -1 || (-n == step)) {
            qnt.innerHTML = Math.round((Number(qnt.innerHTML) + n)*100)/100;
            window.rrAddToBasket(id, qnt.innerHTML);
          }
          if (+qnt.innerHTML == 0) {
            event.target.closest('.rr-item__actions').classList.remove('added');
          }
        }
      }

        getItems(['828219'], function (currentProducts) {
          if (excludedCategoryIds.indexOf(currentProducts[0].CategoryIds[0]) === -1) {
            recoms = recoms.filter(function (item) {
              return excludedCategoryIds.indexOf(item.CategoryIds[0]) === -1;
            });
          }

          var filteredRecoms = recoms
          .filter(function(recom) {
            return recom.Url.indexOf('greensight.ru') == -1
          })
          .filter(function(recom) {
            return excludedProductIds.indexOf(recom.ItemId) == -1;
          })
          .filter(retailrocket.modules.duplicates.filter);

          filteredRecoms.forEach(function(recom) {
            recom.Url = recom.Url.split('/?')[0]
          });

          function renderSpBlock(currentItemId, baseRecoms) {
            retailrocket.impression.forProductPlacement({
              partnerId: retailrocket.api.getPartnerId(),
              placementId: 'fcfd69b8-7720-4298-b0a3-bd334c29ceab',
              session: retailrocket.api.getSessionId(),
              productId: currentItemId,
              callbackContents: {
                'string': function (content) {
                  if (typeof content === 'string') {
                    var spInfoStr = content;
                  } else {
                    var spInfoStr = content.string;
                    impressionContentId = content.id;
                  }

                  var SPinfoParsed = getParsedResponse(spInfoStr);
                  var isRandom = SPinfoParsed.hasOwnProperty('randomProducts');
                  var SPids = isRandom ? SPinfoParsed.randomProducts[getRandomValue(0, SPinfoParsed.randomProducts.length - 1)] : SPinfoParsed.products;

                  getItems(SPids, function(spProducts) {
                    spProducts.forEach(function(recom) {
                      recom.Params.isSpProduct = true;
                    })
                    
                    var spRecoms = filterDouble(spProducts
                    .filter(filterIsAvailable)
                    .concat(baseRecoms)
                    .filter(function(recom) {
                      return String(currentItemId).indexOf(recom.ItemId) === -1;
                    })
                    .filter(retailrocket.modules.duplicates.filter));
                    
                    if (spRecoms.length > 0) {
                      recomTrackSetting.check = true;
                      recomTrackSetting.nameTrack = SPinfoParsed.recomTrack;
                      setStatisticsRender(spRecoms);
                      renderWithClientPreRender('1', spRecoms, renderFn);
                    }
                  });
                },
                'empty': function () {
                  var filteredRecomsMod = baseRecoms;

                  if (filteredRecomsMod.length > 0) {
                    renderWithClientPreRender('1', filteredRecomsMod, renderFn);
                  }
                }
              }
            });
          }

          renderSpBlock(828219, filteredRecoms);
        });
      }
      
      function renderWithClientPreRender (stock, recoms, renderFn) {
        var stockId = Number(stock);
        var data = {
          stock: stockId,
          items:[],
        };

        recoms.forEach(function (item) {
          data.items.push(item.ItemId);
        });

        waitFor(
          function () {
            return window.rrPriceUpdate
          },
          function () {
            rrPriceUpdate(data, function (clientsItems) {
              var parseData = JSON.parse(clientsItems);

              parseData.forEach(function (clientsItem) {
                recoms.forEach(function (recomsItem) {
                  if (clientsItem.gica_id === recomsItem.ItemId) {
                    recomsItem.Price = clientsItem.price;
                    recomsItem.OldPrice = clientsItem.old_price;
                    recomsItem.clientsAvailable = clientsItem.available;
                  }
                });
              });

              recoms = recoms.filter(function (item) {
                return item.clientsAvailable === true;
              });

              if (recoms.length > 0) {
                renderFn(recoms);
              }
            });
          }
        );
      }

      function postRenderFn(widget) {
        waitFor(
          function () {
            return window.swiper
          },
          function () {
            var products = widget.querySelectorAll('.rr-item__sp-product');
            var isShow = false;
            var itemsId = [];
            var rrSwiperCarousel = new SwiperModel({
              widget: widget,
              settingSwiper: {
                wrapperClass: 'rr-swiper-wrapper',
                slideClass: 'rr-swiper-slide',
                init: false,
                updateOnWindowResize: true,
                watchOverflow: true,
                observer: true,
                spaceBetween: 20,
                lazy: true,
                preloadImages: true,
                touchReleaseOnEdges: true,
                watchSlidesVisibility: true,
                loop: true,
                navigation: {
                  prevEl: widget.querySelector('.swiper-prev'),
                  nextEl: widget.querySelector('.swiper-next'),
                },
                autoplay: false,
                speed: 800,
                breakpoints: {
                  1200: {
                    slidesPerView: 4,
                    slidesPerGroup: 1
                  },
                  1024: {
                    slidesPerView: 4,
                    slidesPerGroup: 1
                  },
                  768: {
                    slidesPerView: 4,
                    slidesPerGroup: 1,
                    spaceBetween: 10,
                  },
                  500: {
                    slidesPerView: 3,
                    slidesPerGroup: 1
                  },
                  320: {
                    slidesPerView: 2,
                    slidesPerGroup: 1,
                    spaceBetween: 10,
                  }
                }
              }
            });

            rrSwiperCarousel.getScript();
            
            var productItems = widget.querySelectorAll('.rr-swiper-slide');
            var allProductsArr = [];
			var viewedProductId = [];
            
            productItems.forEach(function(item) {
              var prod = item.querySelector('.rr-item');
              var itemData = {
                'name': prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-name'),
                'id': String(prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-id')),
                'price': Number(prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-price')),
                'brand': prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-brand'),
                'position': prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-position'),
              };

              if (item.classList.contains('swiper-slide-visible')) {
                viewedProductId.push(itemData.id);
                allProductsArr.push(itemData);
              };
              item.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
                var target = event.target;

                if (target.classList.contains('rr-item__title') || target.classList.contains('rr-item__info') || target.classList.contains('rr-item__img')) {
                  dataLayerSend(itemData)
                } else if (target.classList.contains('control-dec') || target.classList.contains('control-inc') || target.closest('.control-inc') != null || target.closest('.control-dec') != null || target.classList.contains('rr-item__actions-buy')) {
                  dataLayerInBasketProduct(itemData)
                }
              })
            })

            dataLayerViewedProducts(allProductsArr);
			
            var oldViewedProductId = viewedProductId;
            
            products.forEach(function(item) {
              itemsId.push(item.getAttribute('data-id'));
            });

            window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
              if (!isShow) {
                var  widgetScrollTop = widget.getBoundingClientRect()['top'];

                if (widgetScrollTop < 150) {
                  setStatisticsShow(itemsId); 
                  isShow = true;
                }
              }
            });
          }
        )
      }

      function dataLayerSend(product) {
        if (typeof dataLayer !== 'undefined') {
          dataLayer.push({
            'event': 'click',
            'ecommerce': {
              'currencyCode': 'RUB', 
              'click': {
                'actionField': {'list': 'rr_product_out_stock'},
                'products': [product]
              }
            },
          });
        }
      }

      function dataLayerViewedProducts(items) {
        var impressionsArr = items;
        
        impressionsArr.forEach(function(view) {
		  view['list'] = 'rr_product_out_stock'
        })
		if (typeof dataLayer !== 'undefined') {
          dataLayer.push({
            'event': 'impressions',
            'ecommerce': {
              'currencyCode': 'RUB', 
              'impressions': impressionsArr
            }
          });
        }
      }
      
      function dataLayerViewProduct(items) {
        items['list'] = 'rr_product_out_stock';
        if (typeof dataLayer !== 'undefined') {
          dataLayer.push({
            'event': 'impressions',
            'ecommerce': {
              'currencyCode': 'RUB', 
              'impressions':  [items],
            },
          });
        }
      }
      
      function dataLayerInBasketProduct(item) {
        item['quantity'] = 1;
        if (typeof dataLayer !== 'undefined') {
          dataLayer.push({
            'event': 'add_to_cart',
            'ecommerce': {
              'currencyCode': 'RUB', 
              'add': {
                'actionField': {'list': 'rr_product_alternative'},
                'products': [item]
              },
            },
          });
        }
      }
      
      return {
        postRenderFn: postRenderFn,
        preRenderFn: preRenderFn,
        setStatisticsClick: setStatisticsClick,
        add2cart: add2cart
      };
    }());

    var widget = document.querySelector('.rr-widget-61e5702f97a52829ecac7bf3-alternative');
    var widgetPosition = widget.getBoundingClientRect()['top'];

    if (widgetPosition < 1000) {
      retailrocket.widget.render('rr-widget-61e5702f97a52829ecac7bf3-alternative');
    } else {
      window.addEventListener('scroll', function widgetRender() {
        var widgetScrollTop = widget.getBoundingClientRect()['top'];
        
        if (widgetScrollTop < 1000) {
          retailrocket.widget.render('rr-widget-61e5702f97a52829ecac7bf3-alternative');
          this.removeEventListener('scroll', widgetRender);
        }
      });
    }
    
  }(retailrocket));

<script type="text/javascript">
  (function (retailrocket) {
    'use strict';

    var waitFor = function (exitCondition, callback, force, opts) {
      var checkCount = (opts && opts.checkCount) || 100;
      var timeout = (opts && opts.timeout) || 1000;

      (function check() {
        var result = exitCondition();
        if (result) {
          callback(result);
          return;
        }

        if (checkCount === 0) {
          if (force) {
            callback();
          }
          return;
        }

        checkCount -= 1;
        setTimeout(check, timeout);
      }());
    };
    
    var SwiperModel = function (setting) {
      var $widget = setting.widget;
      var swiperSeector = '.rr-swiper-container';
      var source = 'https://rrstatic.retailrocket.net/widget/plugins/rrswiper/rrswiper.min.js';
      var itemsCount = $widget.getAttribute('data-number-of-rendered-items');

      function checkloop(paramsSlider) {
        var modSetting = paramsSlider;

        if (modSetting.loop == true) {
          for (var point in modSetting.breakpoints) {
            if (itemsCount <= modSetting.breakpoints[point].slidesPerView) {
              modSetting.breakpoints[point].loop = false;
            } else {
              modSetting.breakpoints[point].loop = true;
            }
          }
        }

        return modSetting;
      }

      function render(swiperLibrary) {
        var SwiperParams = checkloop(setting.settingSwiper);
        var $rrContainer = $widget.querySelector(swiperSeector);
        var rrSwiper = swiperLibrary == 'RRSwiper' ? new RRSwiper($rrContainer, SwiperParams) : new Swiper($rrContainer, SwiperParams);

        rrSwiper
          .on('init', function () {
          var $imgError = $widget.querySelectorAll('.rr-swiper-slide:not(.swiper-slide-duplicate) img');
          var counter = 0;
          var indexImg = [];

          $imgError.forEach(function (img) {
            img.onerror = function () {
              var $slideItem = img.closest('.rr-swiper-slide');
              var $slideSiblings = $slideItem.parentNode.querySelectorAll('.rr-swiper-slide:not(.swiper-slide-duplicate)');
              indexImg.push($slideItem.getAttribute('data-swiper-slide-index'));

              if ($imgError.length == counter) {
                rrSwiper.removeSlide(indexImg);
              }
            };
            counter++;
          });
          $widget.classList.add('rr-active');
        })
          .on('observerUpdate', function () {
          rrSwiper.resize.resizeHandler();
        });
        rrSwiper.init();
      }

      function getScript() {
        var swiperJs = document.createElement('script');
        var getElemScript = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
        swiperJs.async = 1;

        if (!window.Swiper && !window.RRSwiper) {
          swiperJs.onload = swiperJs.onreadystatechange = function(_, isAbort) {
            if (isAbort || !swiperJs.readyState || /loaded|complete/.test(swiperJs.readyState) ) {
              swiperJs.onload = swiperJs.onreadystatechange = null;
              swiperJs = undefined;

              if (!isAbort) setTimeout(render('RRSwiper'), 0);
            }
          };

          swiperJs.src = source;
          getElemScript.parentNode.insertBefore(swiperJs, getElemScript);
        } else {
          var versionSwiper = window.hasOwnProperty('RRSwiper') ? 'RRSwiper' : 'Swiper';
          render(versionSwiper);
        }
      }

      this.getScript = getScript;
    };

    function getItems(requireProducts, callback) {
      retailrocket.items.get(
        retailrocket.api.getPartnerId(),
        requireProducts,
        ['1'],
        callback
      );
    }
    
    function filterDouble(array) {
      var ids = array.map(function (item) {
        return item.ItemId;
      });

      return array.filter(function (item, index) {
        return ids.indexOf(item.ItemId) === index;
      });
    }
    
    if (!('duplicates' in retailrocket.modules)) {
      retailrocket.setModule('duplicates', [], function () {
        var savedIds = [];
        var paramName = 'ItemId';

        function has(id) {
          return savedIds.indexOf(id) !== -1;
        }

        function add(id) {
          savedIds = savedIds.concat(id);
        }

        function remove(id) {
          var ids = [].concat(id);

          savedIds = savedIds.filter(function (savedId) {
            return ids.indexOf(savedId) === -1;
          });
        }

        function filter(recom) {
          if (!recom[paramName]) {
            return true;
          }

          if (!has(recom[paramName])) {
            add(recom[paramName]);
            return true;
          }

          return false;
        }

        function filteredCount(recoms) {
          return recoms.reduce(function (acc, recom) {
            return acc + (has(recom[paramName]) ? 1 : 0);
          }, 0);
        }

        function getItems() {
          return savedIds.slice();
        }

        return {
          has: has,
          add: add,
          remove: remove,
          filter: filter,
          filteredCount: filteredCount,
          getItems: getItems,
        };
      });
    }

      function getParsedResponse(response) {
        var responseMatch = response.match(/{[^}]+}/).toString();

      function getRandomValue(min, max) {

      function add2cart(btn, n, id, step) {
        if (step) {
          n = Number(step) * Number(n);
        }
        var qnt = event.target.closest('.rr-item__actions').querySelector('.control-qnt');
        
        if (btn.classList.contains('rr-item__actions-buy')) {
          btn.closest('.rr-item__actions').classList.add('added');
          qnt.innerHTML = Math.round((Number(qnt.innerHTML) + n)*100)/100;
          window.rrAddToBasket(id, qnt.innerHTML);
        } else {
          if (n == 1 || n == step) {
            qnt.innerHTML = Math.round((Number(qnt.innerHTML) + n)*100)/100;
            window.rrAddToBasket(id, qnt.innerHTML);
          }
          if (n == -1 || (-n == step)) {
            qnt.innerHTML = Math.round((Number(qnt.innerHTML) + n)*100)/100;
            window.rrAddToBasket(id, qnt.innerHTML);
          }
          if (+qnt.innerHTML == 0) {
            event.target.closest('.rr-item__actions').classList.remove('added');
          }
        }
      }

        getItems(['828219'], function (currentProducts) {
          if (excludedCategoryIds.indexOf(currentProducts[0].CategoryIds[0]) === -1) {
            recoms = recoms.filter(function (item) {
              return excludedCategoryIds.indexOf(item.CategoryIds[0]) === -1;
            });
          }

          var filteredRecoms = recoms
          .filter(function(recom) {
            return recom.Url.indexOf('greensight.ru') == -1
          }).filter(function(recom) {
            return excludedProductIds.indexOf(recom.ItemId) == -1;
          })
          .filter(retailrocket.modules.duplicates.filter);

          filteredRecoms.forEach(function(recom) {
            recom.Url = recom.Url.split('/?')[0]
          });

          function renderSpBlock(currentItemId, baseRecoms) {
            retailrocket.impression.forProductPlacement({
              partnerId: retailrocket.api.getPartnerId(),
              placementId: 'fcfd69b8-7720-4298-b0a3-bd334c29ceab',
              session: retailrocket.api.getSessionId(),
              productId: currentItemId,
              callbackContents: {
                'string': function (content) {
                  if (typeof content === 'string') {
                    var spInfoStr = content;
                  } else {
                    var spInfoStr = content.string;
                    impressionContentId = content.id;
                  }

                  var SPinfoParsed = getParsedResponse(spInfoStr);
                  var isRandom = SPinfoParsed.hasOwnProperty('randomProducts');
                  var SPids = isRandom ? SPinfoParsed.randomProducts[getRandomValue(0, SPinfoParsed.randomProducts.length - 1)] : SPinfoParsed.products;

                  getItems(SPids, function(spProducts) {
                    spProducts.forEach(function(recom) {
                      recom.Params.isSpProduct = true;
                    })
                    
                    var spRecoms = filterDouble(spProducts
                    .filter(filterIsAvailable)
                    .concat(baseRecoms)
                    .filter(function(recom) { return String(currentItemId).indexOf(recom.ItemId) === -1 }))
                    //.filter(retailrocket.modules.duplicates.filter);
                    
                    if (spRecoms.length > 0) {
                      recomTrackSetting.check = true;
                      recomTrackSetting.nameTrack = SPinfoParsed.recomTrack;
                      setStatisticsRender(spRecoms);
                      renderWithClientPreRender('1', spRecoms, renderFn);
                    }
                  });
                },
                'empty': function () {
                  var filteredRecomsMod = baseRecoms;

                  if (filteredRecomsMod.length > 0) {
                    renderWithClientPreRender('1', filteredRecomsMod, renderFn);
                  }
                }
              }
            });
          }

          renderSpBlock(828219, filteredRecoms);
        });
      }
      
      function renderWithClientPreRender (stock, recoms, renderFn) {
        var stockId = Number(stock);
        var data = {
          stock: stockId,
          items:[],
        };

        recoms.forEach(function (item) {
          data.items.push(item.ItemId);
        });

        waitFor(
          function () {
            return window.rrPriceUpdate
          },
          function () {
            rrPriceUpdate(data, function (clientsItems) {
              var parseData = JSON.parse(clientsItems);

              parseData.forEach(function (clientsItem) {
                recoms.forEach(function (recomsItem) {
                  if (clientsItem.gica_id === recomsItem.ItemId) {
                    recomsItem.Price = clientsItem.price;
                    recomsItem.OldPrice = clientsItem.old_price;
                    recomsItem.clientsAvailable = clientsItem.available;
                  }
                });
              });

              recoms = recoms.filter(function (item) {
                return item.clientsAvailable === true;
              });

              if (recoms.length > 0) {
                renderFn(recoms);
              }
            });
          }
        );
      }

      function postRenderFn(widget) {
        waitFor(
          function () {
            return window.swiper
          },
          function () {
            var products = widget.querySelectorAll('.rr-item__sp-product');
            var isShow = false;
            var itemsId = [];
            var rrSwiperCarousel = new SwiperModel({
              widget: widget,
              settingSwiper: {
                wrapperClass: 'rr-swiper-wrapper',
                slideClass: 'rr-swiper-slide',
                init: false,
                updateOnWindowResize: true,
                watchOverflow: true,
                observer: true,
                spaceBetween: 20,
                lazy: true,
                on: {
                	slideChange: function () {
                    	var newViewedProductId = [];

                        productItems.forEach(function(item) {
                          var prod = item.querySelector('.rr-item');
                          var itemData = {
                            'name': prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-name'),
                            'id': String(prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-id')),
                            'price': Number(prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-price')),
                            'brand': prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-brand'),
                            'position': prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-position'),
                          };

                          if (item.classList.contains('swiper-slide-visible')) {
                            newViewedProductId.push(itemData.id);
                            if (oldViewedProductId.indexOf(itemData.id) == -1) {
                              dataLayerViewProduct(itemData);
                            }
                          };
                        })

                        oldViewedProductId = newViewedProductId;
                    }
                },
                preloadImages: true,
                touchReleaseOnEdges: true,
                watchSlidesVisibility: true,
                loop: true,
                navigation: {
                  prevEl: widget.querySelector('.swiper-prev'),
                  nextEl: widget.querySelector('.swiper-next'),
                },
                autoplay: false,
                speed: 800,
                breakpoints: {
                  1200: {
                    slidesPerView: 4,
                    slidesPerGroup: 1,
                    allowTouchMove: false
                  },
                  1024: {
                    slidesPerView: 4,
                    slidesPerGroup: 1,
                    allowTouchMove: false
                  },
                  768: {
                    slidesPerView: 4,
                    slidesPerGroup: 1,
                    spaceBetween: 10,
                    allowTouchMove: true
                  },
                  500: {
                    slidesPerView: 3,
                    slidesPerGroup: 1,
                    allowTouchMove: true
                  },
                  320: {
                    slidesPerView: 2,
                    slidesPerGroup: 1,
                    spaceBetween: 10,
                    allowTouchMove: true
                  }
                }
              }
            });

            rrSwiperCarousel.getScript();
            
            var productItems = widget.querySelectorAll('.rr-swiper-slide');
            var allProductsArr = [];
			var viewedProductId = [];
            
            
            productItems.forEach(function(item) {
              var prod = item.querySelector('.rr-item');
              var itemData = {
                'name': prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-name'),
                'id': String(prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-id')),
                'price': Number(prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-price')),
                'brand': prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-brand'),
                'position': prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-position'),
              };

              if (item.classList.contains('swiper-slide-visible')) {
                viewedProductId.push(itemData.id);
                allProductsArr.push(itemData);
              };
              item.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
                var target = event.target;

                if (target.classList.contains('rr-item__title') || target.classList.contains('rr-item__info') || target.classList.contains('rr-item__img')) {
                  dataLayerSend(itemData);
                } else if (target.classList.contains('control-inc') || target.closest('.control-inc') != null || target.classList.contains('rr-item__actions-buy')) {
                  dataLayerInBasketProduct(itemData);
                } else if (target.classList.contains('control-dec') || target.closest('.control-dec') != null || target.classList.contains('rr-item__actions-buy')) {
                  dataLayerRemoveFromBasketProduct(itemData);
                }
              })
            })

            dataLayerViewedProducts(allProductsArr);
			
            var oldViewedProductId = viewedProductId;
            
            products.forEach(function(item) {
              itemsId.push(item.getAttribute('data-id'));
            });

            window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
              if (!isShow) {
                var  widgetScrollTop = widget.getBoundingClientRect()['top'];

                if (widgetScrollTop < 150) {
                  setStatisticsShow(itemsId); 
                  isShow = true;
                }
              }
            });
          }
        )
      }

      function dataLayerSend(product) {
        dataLayer.push({
          'event': 'click',
          'ecommerce': {
            'currencyCode': 'RUB', 
            'click': {
              'actionField': {'list': 'rr_product_alternative'},
              'products': [product]
            }
          },
        });
      }

      function dataLayerViewedProducts(items) {
        var impressionsArr = items;
        
        impressionsArr.forEach(function(view) {
		  view['list'] = 'rr_product_alternative'
        })

        dataLayer.push({
          'event': 'impressions',
          'ecommerce': {
            'currencyCode': 'RUB', 
            'impressions': impressionsArr
          }
        });
      }
      
      function dataLayerViewProduct(items) {
        items['list'] = 'rr_product_alternative';
        
        dataLayer.push({
          'event': 'impressions',
          'ecommerce': {
            'currencyCode': 'RUB', 
            'impressions':  [items],
          },
        });
      }
      
      function dataLayerInBasketProduct(item) {
        item['quantity'] = 1;
        
        dataLayer.push({
          'event': 'add_to_cart',
          'ecommerce': {
            'currencyCode': 'RUB', 
            'add': {
              'actionField': {'list': 'rr_product_alternative'},
              'products': [item]
            },
          },
        });
      }
      
      function dataLayerRemoveFromBasketProduct(item) {
        item['quantity'] = 1;
        
        dataLayer.push({
          'event': 'removeFromCart',
          'ecommerce': {
            'currencyCode': 'RUB', 
            'remove': {
              'actionField': {'list': 'rr_main_personal'},
              'products': [item]
            },
          },
        });
      }
      
      return {
        postRenderFn: postRenderFn,
        preRenderFn: preRenderFn,
        setStatisticsClick: setStatisticsClick,
        add2cart: add2cart
      };
    }());

    var widget = document.querySelector('.rr-widget-5ede0b6097a52530444d9c53-alternative');
    var widgetPosition = widget.getBoundingClientRect()['top'];

    if (widgetPosition < 1000) {
      retailrocket.widget.render('rr-widget-5ede0b6097a52530444d9c53-alternative');
    } else {
      window.addEventListener('scroll', function widgetRender() {
        var widgetScrollTop = widget.getBoundingClientRect()['top'];
        
        if (widgetScrollTop < 1000) {
          retailrocket.widget.render('rr-widget-5ede0b6097a52530444d9c53-alternative');
          this.removeEventListener('scroll', widgetRender);
        }
      });
    }
    
  }(retailrocket));

<script type="text/javascript">
  (function (retailrocket) {
    'use strict';

    var waitFor = function (exitCondition, callback, force, opts) {
      var checkCount = (opts && opts.checkCount) || 100;
      var timeout = (opts && opts.timeout) || 1000;

      (function check() {
        var result = exitCondition();
        if (result) {
          callback(result);
          return;
        }

        if (checkCount === 0) {
          if (force) {
            callback();
          }
          return;
        }

        checkCount -= 1;
        setTimeout(check, timeout);
      }());
    };
    
    var SwiperModel = function (setting) {
      var $widget = setting.widget;
      var swiperSeector = '.rr-swiper-container';
      var source = 'https://rrstatic.retailrocket.net/widget/plugins/rrswiper/rrswiper.min.js';
      var itemsCount = $widget.getAttribute('data-number-of-rendered-items');

      function checkloop(paramsSlider) {
        var modSetting = paramsSlider;

        if (modSetting.loop == true) {
          for (var point in modSetting.breakpoints) {
            if (itemsCount <= modSetting.breakpoints[point].slidesPerView) {
              modSetting.breakpoints[point].loop = false;
            } else {
              modSetting.breakpoints[point].loop = true;
            }
          }
        }

        return modSetting;
      }

      function render(swiperLibrary) {
        var SwiperParams = checkloop(setting.settingSwiper);
        var $rrContainer = $widget.querySelector(swiperSeector);
        var rrSwiper = swiperLibrary == 'RRSwiper' ? new RRSwiper($rrContainer, SwiperParams) : new Swiper($rrContainer, SwiperParams);

        rrSwiper
          .on('init', function () {
          var $imgError = $widget.querySelectorAll('.rr-swiper-slide:not(.swiper-slide-duplicate) img');
          var counter = 0;
          var indexImg = [];

          $imgError.forEach(function (img) {
            img.onerror = function () {
              var $slideItem = img.closest('.rr-swiper-slide');
              var $slideSiblings = $slideItem.parentNode.querySelectorAll('.rr-swiper-slide:not(.swiper-slide-duplicate)');
              indexImg.push($slideItem.getAttribute('data-swiper-slide-index'));

              if ($imgError.length == counter) {
                rrSwiper.removeSlide(indexImg);
              }
            };
            counter++;
          });
          $widget.classList.add('rr-active');
        })
          .on('observerUpdate', function () {
          rrSwiper.resize.resizeHandler();
        });
        rrSwiper.init();
      }

      function getScript() {
        var swiperJs = document.createElement('script');
        var getElemScript = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
        swiperJs.async = 1;

        if (!window.Swiper && !window.RRSwiper) {
          swiperJs.onload = swiperJs.onreadystatechange = function(_, isAbort) {
            if (isAbort || !swiperJs.readyState || /loaded|complete/.test(swiperJs.readyState) ) {
              swiperJs.onload = swiperJs.onreadystatechange = null;
              swiperJs = undefined;

              if (!isAbort) setTimeout(render('RRSwiper'), 0);
            }
          };

          swiperJs.src = source;
          getElemScript.parentNode.insertBefore(swiperJs, getElemScript);
        } else {
          var versionSwiper = window.hasOwnProperty('RRSwiper') ? 'RRSwiper' : 'Swiper';
          render(versionSwiper);
        }
      }

      this.getScript = getScript;
    };

    function getItems(requireProducts, callback) {
      retailrocket.items.get(
        retailrocket.api.getPartnerId(),
        requireProducts,
        ['1'],
        callback
      );
    }
    
    function filterDouble(array) {
      var ids = array.map(function (item) {
        return item.ItemId;
      });

      return array.filter(function (item, index) {
        return ids.indexOf(item.ItemId) === index;
      });
    }
    
    if (!('duplicates' in retailrocket.modules)) {
      retailrocket.setModule('duplicates', [], function () {
        var savedIds = [];
        var paramName = 'ItemId';

        function has(id) {
          return savedIds.indexOf(id) !== -1;
        }

        function add(id) {
          savedIds = savedIds.concat(id);
        }

        function remove(id) {
          var ids = [].concat(id);

          savedIds = savedIds.filter(function (savedId) {
            return ids.indexOf(savedId) === -1;
          });
        }

        function filter(recom) {
          if (!recom[paramName]) {
            return true;
          }

          if (!has(recom[paramName])) {
            add(recom[paramName]);
            return true;
          }

          return false;
        }

        function filteredCount(recoms) {
          return recoms.reduce(function (acc, recom) {
            return acc + (has(recom[paramName]) ? 1 : 0);
          }, 0);
        }

        function getItems() {
          return savedIds.slice();
        }

        return {
          has: has,
          add: add,
          remove: remove,
          filter: filter,
          filteredCount: filteredCount,
          getItems: getItems,
        };
      });
    }

    retailrocket['auchan5ede0b6b97a52530444d9c54'] = (function () {
      var list = 'rr_product_related';
      var recomTrackSetting = {
        nameTrack: '',
        abSegment: '',
        check: false,
        listTrack: function()
        {
          return [this.nameTrack, this.nameTrack + 'Card'];
        },
      };
      var impressionContentId = null;

      function setStatisticsRender(recoms) {
        if (recomTrackSetting.check) {
          var itemsId = recoms.map(function(product) { return product.ItemId });

          recomTrackSetting.listTrack().forEach(function(track) {
            rrApiOnReady.push(function() {
              rrApi.recomTrack(
                '5ede0b6b97a52530444d9c54',
                0,
                [itemsId],
                {
                  eventType: 'blockRender',
                  abtest: recomTrackSetting.abSegment,
                  algorithm: track
                }
              );
            });
          });
        }
      }

      function setStatisticsShow(recomIds) {
        if (recomTrackSetting.check) {
          recomTrackSetting.listTrack().forEach(function(track) {
            rrApiOnReady.push(function() {
              rrApi.recomTrack(
                '5ede0b6b97a52530444d9c54',
                0,
                [recomIds],
                {
                  eventType: 'blockView',
                  abtest: recomTrackSetting.abSegment,
                  algorithm: track
                }
              );
            });
          });

          if (impressionContentId !== null) {
            rrApi.impressionContentViewed({
              impressionContentId: impressionContentId,
              onSuccessCallback: function() {}
            });
          }
        }
      }

      function setStatisticsClick(itemId) {
        if (recomTrackSetting.check) {
          recomTrackSetting.listTrack().forEach(function(track) {
            rrApiOnReady.push(function() {
              rrApi.recomTrack(
                '5ede0b6b97a52530444d9c54',
                0,
                [],
                {
                  eventType: 'blockClick',
                  clickedItem: itemId,
                  abtest: recomTrackSetting.abSegment,
                  algorithm: track
                }
              );
            });
          });

          if (impressionContentId !== null) {
            rrApi.impressionContentClicked({
              impressionContentId: impressionContentId,
              onSuccessCallback: function() {}
            });
          }
        }
      }
      
      function getParsedResponse(response) {
        var responseMatch = response.match(/{[^}]+}/).toString();
        var responseParsed = JSON.parse(responseMatch.replace(/([a-zA-Z]+):/g,'"$1":'));

        return responseParsed;
      }

      function getRandomValue(min, max) {
        return Math.round(Math.random() * (max - min) + min);
      }
      
      function filterIsAvailable(recom) {
        return recom.IsAvailable === true;
      }
      
      function getItems(requireProducts, callback) {
        retailrocket.items.get(
          retailrocket.api.getPartnerId(),
          requireProducts,
          ['1'],
          callback
        );
      }
      
      function add2cart(btn, n, id, step) {
        if (step) {
          n = Number(step) * Number(n);
        }
        var qnt = event.target.closest('.rr-item__actions').querySelector('.control-qnt');
        
        if (btn.classList.contains('rr-item__actions-buy')) {
          btn.closest('.rr-item__actions').classList.add('added');
          qnt.innerHTML = Math.round((Number(qnt.innerHTML) + n)*100)/100;
          window.rrAddToBasket(id, qnt.innerHTML);
        } else {
          if (n == 1 || n == step) {
            qnt.innerHTML = Math.round((Number(qnt.innerHTML) + n)*100)/100;
            window.rrAddToBasket(id, qnt.innerHTML);
          }
          if (n == -1 || (-n == step)) {
            qnt.innerHTML = Math.round((Number(qnt.innerHTML) + n)*100)/100;
            window.rrAddToBasket(id, qnt.innerHTML);
          }
          if (+qnt.innerHTML == 0) {
            event.target.closest('.rr-item__actions').classList.remove('added');
          }
        }
      }

            recoms = recoms.filter(function (item) {
              return excludedCategoryIds.indexOf(item.CategoryIds[0]) === -1;
            });
          }

          var filteredRecoms = recoms
          .filter(function(recom) {
            return recom.Url.indexOf('greensight.ru') == -1;
          })
          .filter(function(recom) {
            return excludedProductIds.indexOf(recom.ItemId) == -1;

          });

          function renderSpBlock(currentItemId, baseRecoms) {
            retailrocket.impression.forProductPlacement({
              partnerId: retailrocket.api.getPartnerId(),
              placementId: 'b3299782-c150-4cf1-9218-558f3af73d0b',
              session: retailrocket.api.getSessionId(),
              productId: currentItemId,
              callbackContents: {
                'string': function (content) {
                  if (typeof content === 'string') {
                    var spInfoStr = content;
                  } else {
                    var spInfoStr = content.string;
                    impressionContentId = content.id;
                  }

                  var SPinfoParsed = getParsedResponse(spInfoStr);
                  var isRandom = SPinfoParsed.hasOwnProperty('randomProducts');
                  var SPids = isRandom ? SPinfoParsed.randomProducts[getRandomValue(0, SPinfoParsed.randomProducts.length - 1)] : SPinfoParsed.products;

                  getItems(SPids, function(spProducts) {
                    spProducts.forEach(function(recom) {
                      recom.Params.isSpProduct = true;
                    })

                    var spRecoms = filterDouble(spProducts
                    .filter(filterIsAvailable)
                    .concat(baseRecoms)
                    .filter(function(recom) {
                      return String(currentItemId).indexOf(recom.ItemId) === -1
                    })
                    .filter(retailrocket.modules.duplicates.filter));
                    

                    if (spRecoms.length > 0) {
                      recomTrackSetting.check = true;
                      recomTrackSetting.nameTrack = SPinfoParsed.recomTrack;
                      setStatisticsRender(spRecoms);
                      list = 'rr_product_related-SP';

                      renderWithClientPreRender('1', spRecoms, renderFn);
                    }
                  });
                },
                'empty': function () {
                  var filteredRecomsMod = baseRecoms.filter(retailrocket.modules.duplicates.filter);

                  if (filteredRecomsMod.length > 0) {
                    renderWithClientPreRender('1', filteredRecomsMod, renderFn);
                  }
                }
              }
            });
          }

          renderSpBlock('828219', filteredRecoms);
        })
      }
      
      function renderWithClientPreRender (stock, recoms, renderFn) {
        var stockId = Number(stock);
        var data = {
          stock: stockId,
          items:[],
        };

        recoms.forEach(function (item) {
          data.items.push(item.ItemId);
        });
        
        waitFor(
          function () {
            return window.rrPriceUpdate
          },
          function () {
            rrPriceUpdate(data, function (clientsItems) {
              var parseData = JSON.parse(clientsItems);

              parseData.forEach(function (clientsItem) {
                recoms.forEach(function (recomsItem) {
                  if (clientsItem.gica_id === recomsItem.ItemId) {
                    recomsItem.Price = clientsItem.price;
                    recomsItem.OldPrice = clientsItem.old_price;
                    recomsItem.clientsAvailable = clientsItem.available;
                  }
                });
              });

              recoms = recoms.filter(function (item) {
                return item.clientsAvailable === true;
              });

              if (recoms.length > 0) {
                renderFn(recoms);
              }
            });
          }
        );
      }

      function postRenderFn(widget) {
        waitFor(
          function () {
            return window.swiper
          },
          function () {
            var products = widget.querySelectorAll('.rr-item__sp-product');
            var isShow = false;
            var itemsId = [];
            var rrSwiperCarousel = new SwiperModel({
              widget: widget,
              settingSwiper: {
                wrapperClass: 'rr-swiper-wrapper',
                slideClass: 'rr-swiper-slide',
                init: false,
                updateOnWindowResize: true,
                watchOverflow: true,
                observer: true,
                spaceBetween: 20,
                lazy: true,
                on: {
                	slideChange: function () {
                    	var newViewedProductId = [];

                        productItems.forEach(function(item) {
                          var prod = item.querySelector('.rr-item');
                          var itemData = {
                            'name': prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-name'),
                            'id': String(prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-id')),
                            'price': Number(prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-price')),
                            'brand': prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-brand'),
                            'position': prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-position'),
                          };

                          if (item.classList.contains('swiper-slide-visible')) {
                            newViewedProductId.push(itemData.id);
                            if (oldViewedProductId.indexOf(itemData.id) == -1) {
                              dataLayerViewProduct(itemData);
                            }
                          };
                        })
                        oldViewedProductId = newViewedProductId;
                    }
                },
                preloadImages: true,
                touchReleaseOnEdges: true,
                watchSlidesVisibility: true,
                loop: true,
                navigation: {
                  prevEl: widget.querySelector('.swiper-prev'),
                  nextEl: widget.querySelector('.swiper-next'),
                },
                autoplay: false,
                speed: 800,
                breakpoints: {
                  1200: {
                    slidesPerView: 4,
                    slidesPerGroup: 1,
                    allowTouchMove: false
                  },
                  1024: {
                    slidesPerView: 4,
                    slidesPerGroup: 1,
                    allowTouchMove: false
                  },
                  768: {
                    slidesPerView: 4,
                    slidesPerGroup: 1,
                    spaceBetween: 10,
                    allowTouchMove: true
                  },
                  500: {
                    slidesPerView: 3,
                    slidesPerGroup: 1,
                    allowTouchMove: true
                  },
                  320: {
                    slidesPerView: 2,
                    slidesPerGroup: 1,
                    spaceBetween: 10,
                    allowTouchMove: true
                  }
                }
              }
            });

            rrSwiperCarousel.getScript();
            
            var productItems = widget.querySelectorAll('.rr-swiper-slide');
            var allProductsArr = [];
			var viewedProductId = [];
            
            productItems.forEach(function(item) {
              var prod = item.querySelector('.rr-item');
              var itemData = {
                'name': prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-name'),
                'id': String(prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-id')),
                'price': Number(prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-price')),
                'brand': prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-brand'),
                'position': prod.getAttribute('rr-ga-position'),
              };
              
              if (item.classList.contains('swiper-slide-visible')) {
                viewedProductId.push(itemData.id);
                allProductsArr.push(itemData);
              };
              item.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
                var target = event.target;

                if (target.classList.contains('rr-item__title') || target.classList.contains('rr-item__info') || target.classList.contains('rr-item__img')) {
                  dataLayerSend(itemData);
                } else if (target.classList.contains('control-inc') || target.closest('.control-inc') != null || target.classList.contains('rr-item__actions-buy')) {
                  dataLayerInBasketProduct(itemData);
                } else if (target.classList.contains('control-dec') || target.closest('.control-dec') != null || target.classList.contains('rr-item__actions-buy')) {
                  dataLayerRemoveFromBasketProduct(itemData);
                }
              })
            })

            dataLayerViewedProducts(allProductsArr);
			
            var oldViewedProductId = viewedProductId;

            products.forEach(function(item) {
              itemsId.push(item.getAttribute('data-id'));
            });

            window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
              if (!isShow) {
                var  widgetScrollTop = widget.getBoundingClientRect()['top'];

                if (widgetScrollTop < 150) {
                  setStatisticsShow(itemsId); 
                  isShow = true;
                }
              }
            });
          }
        )
      }

      function dataLayerSend(product) {
        dataLayer.push({
          'event': 'click',
          'ecommerce': {
            'currencyCode': 'RUB', 
            'click': {
              'actionField': {'list': list},
              'products': [product]
            }
          },
        });
      }

      function dataLayerViewedProducts(items) {
        var impressionsArr = items;
        
        impressionsArr.forEach(function(view) {
		  view['list'] = list;
        })

        dataLayer.push({
          'event': 'impressions',
          'ecommerce': {
            'currencyCode': 'RUB', 
            'impressions': impressionsArr
          }
        });
      }
      
      function dataLayerViewProduct(items) {
        items['list'] = list;
        
        dataLayer.push({
          'event': 'impressions',
          'ecommerce': {
            'currencyCode': 'RUB', 
            'impressions':  [items],
          },
        });
      }
      
      function dataLayerInBasketProduct(item) {
        item['quantity'] = 1;
        
        dataLayer.push({
          'event': 'add_to_cart',
          'ecommerce': {
            'currencyCode': 'RUB', 
            'add': {
              'actionField': {'list': list},
              'products': [item]
            },
          },
        });
      }
      
      function dataLayerRemoveFromBasketProduct(item) {
        item['quantity'] = 1;
        
        dataLayer.push({
          'event': 'removeFromCart',
          'ecommerce': {
            'currencyCode': 'RUB', 
            'remove': {
              'actionField': {'list': list},
              'products': [item]
            },
          },
        });
      }
      
      return {
        postRenderFn: postRenderFn,
        preRenderFn: preRenderFn,
        setStatisticsClick: setStatisticsClick,
        add2cart: add2cart
      };
    }());

    var widget = document.querySelector('.rr-widget-5ede0b6b97a52530444d9c54-related');
    var widgetPosition = widget.getBoundingClientRect()['top'];

    if (widgetPosition < 1000) {
      retailrocket.widget.render('rr-widget-5ede0b6b97a52530444d9c54-related');
    } else {
      window.addEventListener('scroll', function widgetRender() {
        var widgetScrollTop = widget.getBoundingClientRect()['top'];
        
        if (widgetScrollTop < 1000) {
          retailrocket.widget.render('rr-widget-5ede0b6b97a52530444d9c54-related');
          this.removeEventListener('scroll', widgetRender);
        }
      });
    }
    
  }(retailrocket));
